   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){
                 $('#login-form').submit(function(e){
                     e.preventDefault();
 
                     var loginform = $('#login-form');
                     var action = loginform.attr('action');
                     var datas = loginform.serialize();
 
                     // Post data to login.
                     $.post(
                             action,
                             datas,
                             function(resp){
                                 if(resp.login=='success'){
                                     $('#ajax-response').html('<p class="alert-success">Login Success</p>');
                                     location.reload();
                                 }else{
                                     $('#ajax-response').html('<p class="alert-danger">' + resp.login + '</p>');
                                 }
                             },
                             'json'
                     );
                 });
             });
   </script>
